			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json') !== '18289759e668aaab6463453b60d000b8943926a4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
		}
	}
}
